<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the range slider package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> rangeSlider</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/slider&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>The range slider package exports two key functions:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - State machine logic.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
</ul>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Pass a unique <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">useMachine</code> so generated element ids stay predictable.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Then use the framework integration helpers:</p>

</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token script"><span class="token language-javascript">  <span class="token keyword">const</span> api <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">computed</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> slider<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">connect</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>service<span class="token punctuation">,</span> normalizeProps<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag">        <span class="token attr-name">:key</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span>index<span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span></span>

<h2 id="changing-the-orientation" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Changing the orientation<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#changing-the-orientation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>By default, the slider is assumed to be horizontal. To change the orientation to
vertical, set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">orientation</code> property in the machine&#x27;s context to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">vertical</code>.</p>
<p>In this mode, the slider will use the arrow up and down keys to
increment/decrement its value.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Don&#x27;t forget to change the styles of the vertical slider by specifying its
height</p>
</blockquote>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>rangeSlider<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">orientation</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;vertical&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="setting-the-initial-value" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Setting the initial value<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-initial-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>rangeSlider<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">defaultValue</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">30</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">60</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="controlled-range-value" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Controlled range value<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlled-range-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code> to control both thumb values externally.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>rangeSlider<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  value<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onValueChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">setValue</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">value</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="specifying-the-minimum-and-maximum" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Specifying the minimum and maximum<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#specifying-the-minimum-and-maximum"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>By default, the minimum is <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">0</code> and the maximum is <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">100</code>. If that&#x27;s not what you
want, you can easily specify different bounds by changing the values of the min
and/or max attributes.</p>
<p>For example, to ask the user for a value between <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">-10</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">10</code>, you can use:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>rangeSlider<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">min</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">max</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="setting-the-values-granularity" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Setting the value&#x27;s granularity<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-values-granularity"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>By default, the granularity, is <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">1</code>, meaning that the value is always an
integer. You can change the step attribute to control the granularity.</p>
<p>For example, If you need a value between <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">5</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">10</code>, accurate to two decimal
places, you should set the value of step to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">0.01</code>:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>rangeSlider<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">min</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">5</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">max</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">step</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0.01</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="listening-for-changes" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Listening for changes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-changes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>When the slider value changes, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChangeEnd</code>
callbacks are invoked. You can use this to setup custom behaviors in your app.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>rangeSlider<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">onValueChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { value: number[] }</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;value changing to:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">value</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">onValueChangeEnd</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { value: number[] }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;value has changed to:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">value</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="listening-for-thumb-focus-changes" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Listening for thumb focus changes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-thumb-focus-changes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onFocusChange</code> to track which thumb is currently focused.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>rangeSlider<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onFocusChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { focusedIndex: number, value: number[] }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;focused thumb:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">focusedIndex</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="preventing-thumb-overlap" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Preventing thumb overlap<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#preventing-thumb-overlap"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>By default, the range slider thumbs are allowed to overlap when their values are
equal. To prevent this, use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">minStepsBetweenThumbs</code> to avoid thumbs with
equal values.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>rangeSlider<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">minStepsBetweenThumbs</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="thumb-collision-behavior" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Thumb collision behavior<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#thumb-collision-behavior"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">thumbCollisionBehavior</code> to control how thumbs behave on collision.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>rangeSlider<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">defaultValue</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">80</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">thumbCollisionBehavior</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;push&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token comment">// &quot;none&quot; | &quot;push&quot; | &quot;swap&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="usage-within-forms" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage within forms<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage-within-forms"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>To use range slider in forms, set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">name</code> and render
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.getHiddenInputProps({ index })</code> for each thumb.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>rangeSlider<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">name</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;quantity&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="rtl-support" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">RTL Support<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#rtl-support"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>The slider has built-in support for RTL alignment and interaction. In the RTL
mode, operations are performed from right to left, meaning, the left arrow key
will increment and the right arrow key will decrement.</p>
<p>To enable RTL support, pass the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dir: rtl</code> context property</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>rangeSlider<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">dir</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;rtl&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>While we take care of the interactions in RTL mode, you&#x27;ll have to ensure you
apply the correct CSS styles to flip the layout.</p>
</blockquote>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each slider part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<h3 id="focused-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Focused State<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#focused-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the slider thumb is focused, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-focus</code> attribute is added to the
root, control, thumb and label parts.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-focus</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;thumb&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token pseudo-class">:focus</span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for thumb focus state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;control&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-focus</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for control focus state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;track&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-focus</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;range&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-focus</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for range focus state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="disabled-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabled State<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabled-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the slider is disabled, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-disabled</code> attribute is added to the root,
label, control and thumb.</p>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;control&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

<h3 id="orientation" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Orientation<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#orientation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-orientation</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;(horizontal|vertical)&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;thumb&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-orientation</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;(horizontal|vertical)&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The slider machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ root: string; thumb: (index: number) =&gt; string; hiddenInput: (index: number) =&gt; string; control: string; track: string; range: string; label: string; valueText: string; marker: (index: number) =&gt; string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the elements in the slider. Useful for composition.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">aria-label</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string[]</code><span class="d_block">The aria-label of each slider thumb. Useful for providing an accessible name to the slider</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">aria-labelledby</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string[]</code><span class="d_block">The `id` of the elements that labels each slider thumb. Useful for providing an accessible name to the slider</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">name</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The name associated with each slider thumb (when used in a form)</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">form</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The associate form of the underlying input element.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number[]</code><span class="d_block">The controlled value of the slider</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number[]</code><span class="d_block">The initial value of the slider when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the value of the slider.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disabled</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the slider is disabled</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">readOnly</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the slider is read-only</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">invalid</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the slider is invalid</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: ValueChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function invoked when the value of the slider changes</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChangeEnd</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: ValueChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function invoked when the slider value change is done</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onFocusChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: FocusChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function invoked when the slider&#x27;s focused index changes</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getAriaValueText</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: ValueTextDetails) =&gt; string</code><span class="d_block">Function that returns a human readable value for the slider thumb</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">min</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The minimum value of the slider</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">max</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The maximum value of the slider</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">step</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The step value of the slider</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">minStepsBetweenThumbs</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The minimum permitted steps between multiple thumbs.

`minStepsBetweenThumbs` * `step` should reflect the gap between the thumbs.

- `step: 1` and `minStepsBetweenThumbs: 10` =&gt; gap is `10`
- `step: 10` and `minStepsBetweenThumbs: 2` =&gt; gap is `20`</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">orientation</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;vertical&quot; | &quot;horizontal&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The orientation of the slider</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">origin</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;start&quot; | &quot;center&quot; | &quot;end&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The origin of the slider range. The track is filled from the origin
to the thumb for single values.
- &quot;start&quot;: Useful when the value represents an absolute value
- &quot;center&quot;: Useful when the value represents an offset (relative)
- &quot;end&quot;: Useful when the value represents an offset from the end</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">thumbAlignment</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;center&quot; | &quot;contain&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The alignment of the slider thumb relative to the track
- `center`: the thumb will extend beyond the bounds of the slider track.
- `contain`: the thumb will be contained within the bounds of the track.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">thumbSize</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">{ width: number; height: number; }</code><span class="d_block">The slider thumbs dimensions</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">thumbCollisionBehavior</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;none&quot; | &quot;push&quot; | &quot;swap&quot;</code><span class="d_block">Controls how thumbs behave when they collide during pointer interactions.
- `none` (default): Thumbs cannot move past each other; excess movement is ignored.
- `push`: Thumbs push each other without restoring their previous positions when dragged back.
- `swap`: Thumbs swap places when dragged past each other.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dir</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;ltr&quot; | &quot;rtl&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The document&#x27;s text/writing direction.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The unique identifier of the machine.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getRootNode</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; ShadowRoot | Node | Document</code><span class="d_block">A root node to correctly resolve document in custom environments. E.x.: Iframes, Electron.</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The slider <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number[]</code><span class="d_block">The value of the slider.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dragging</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the slider is being dragged.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">focused</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the slider is focused.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">setValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(value: number[]) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to set the value of the slider.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getThumbValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(index: number) =&gt; number</code><span class="d_block">Returns the value of the thumb at the given index.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">setThumbValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(index: number, value: number) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Sets the value of the thumb at the given index.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getValuePercent</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(value: number) =&gt; number</code><span class="d_block">Returns the percent of the thumb at the given index.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getPercentValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(percent: number) =&gt; number</code><span class="d_block">Returns the value of the thumb at the given percent.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getThumbPercent</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(index: number) =&gt; number</code><span class="d_block">Returns the percent of the thumb at the given index.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">setThumbPercent</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(index: number, percent: number) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Sets the percent of the thumb at the given index.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getThumbMin</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(index: number) =&gt; number</code><span class="d_block">Returns the min value of the thumb at the given index.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getThumbMax</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(index: number) =&gt; number</code><span class="d_block">Returns the max value of the thumb at the given index.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">increment</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(index: number) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to increment the value of the slider at the given index.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">decrement</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(index: number) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to decrement the value of the slider at the given index.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">focus</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">VoidFunction</code><span class="d_block">Function to focus the slider. This focuses the first thumb.</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="data-attributes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Data Attributes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#data-attributes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_8px pl_0! li-t_none li-pos_inside dvd-y_1px"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_4 py_4"><div class="fw_semibold">Label</div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column bdr_3px">data-part</kbd></div><span>label</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-orientation</kbd></div><span>The orientation of the label</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono bdr_3px">data-focus</kbd></div><span>Present when focused</span></div></div></div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_4 py_4"><div class="fw_semibold">Root</div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column <h2 id="accessibility" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Accessibility<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Adheres to the
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/slidertwothumb" class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px">Slider WAI-ARIA design pattern</a>.</p>
<h3 id="keyboard-interactions" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Keyboard Interactions<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#keyboard-interactions"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>

range slider is a multi-thumb slider used to select a range between two\nnumbers.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cresources pkg=\"@zag-js/slider\"\u003e\n\u003cshowcase id=\"RangeSlider\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFeatures\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eFully managed keyboard navigation\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports touch or click on track to update value\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports Right-to-Left directionality\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports horizontal and vertical orientations\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePrevents text selection while dragging\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eInstallation\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eInstall the range slider package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"range-slider/installation.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eAnatomy\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eCheck the slider anatomy and part names.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eEach part includes a \u003ccode\u003edata-part\u003c/code\u003e attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003canatomy id=\"slider\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eUsage\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eImport the range slider package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003eimport * as rangeSlider from \"@zag-js/slider\"\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe range slider package exports two key functions:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003emachine\u003c/code\u003e - State machine logic.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003econnect\u003c/code\u003e - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003ePass a unique \u003ccode\u003eid\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003euseMachine\u003c/code\u003e so generated element ids stay predictable.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThen use the framework integration helpers:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"range-slider/usage.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eChanging the orientation\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBy default, the slider is assumed to be horizontal. To change the orientation to\nvertical, set the \u003ccode\u003eorientation\u003c/code\u003e property in the machine's context to \u003ccode\u003evertical\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eIn this mode, the slider will use the arrow up and down keys to\nincrement/decrement its value.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eDon't forget to change the styles of the vertical slider by specifying its\nheight\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(rangeSlider.machine, {\n  orientation: \"vertical\",\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eSetting the initial value\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(rangeSlider.machine, {\n  defaultValue: [30, 60],\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eControlled range value\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003evalue\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eonValueChange\u003c/code\u003e to control both thumb values externally.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(rangeSlider.machine, {\n  value,\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    setValue(details.value)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eSpecifying the minimum and maximum\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBy default, the minimum is \u003ccode\u003e0\u003c/code\u003e and the maximum is \u003ccode\u003e100\u003c/code\u003e. If that's not what you\nwant, you can easily specify different bounds by changing the values of the min\nand/or max attributes.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eFor example, to ask the user for a value between \u003ccode\u003e-10\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003e10\u003c/code\u003e, you can use:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2-3}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(rangeSlider.machine, {\n  min: -10,\n  max: 10,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eSetting the value's granularity\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBy default, the granularity, is \u003ccode\u003e1\u003c/code\u003e, meaning that the value is always an\ninteger. You can change the step attribute to control the granularity.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eFor example, If you need a value between \u003ccode\u003e5\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003e10\u003c/code\u003e, accurate to two decimal\nplaces, you should set the value of step to \u003ccode\u003e0.01\u003c/code\u003e:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{4}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(rangeSlider.machine, {\n  min: 5,\n  max: 10,\n  step: 0.01,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eListening for changes\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen the slider value changes, the \u003ccode\u003eonValueChange\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eonValueChangeEnd\u003c/code\u003e\ncallbacks are invoked. You can use this to setup custom behaviors in your app.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2-7}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(rangeSlider.machine, {\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: number[] }\n    console.log(\"value changing to:\", details.value)\n  },\n  onValueChangeEnd(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: number[] }\n    console.log(\"value has changed to:\", details.value)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eListening for thumb focus changes\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003eonFocusChange\u003c/code\u003e to track which thumb is currently focused.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(rangeSlider.machine, {\n  onFocusChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { focusedIndex: number, value: number[] }\n    console.log(\"focused thumb:\", details.focusedIndex)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003ePreventing thumb overlap\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBy default, the range slider thumbs are allowed to overlap when their values are\nequal. To prevent this, use the \u003ccode\u003eminStepsBetweenThumbs\u003c/code\u003e to avoid thumbs with\nequal values.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(rangeSlider.machine, {\n  minStepsBetweenThumbs: 1,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eThumb collision behavior\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003ethumbCollisionBehavior\u003c/code\u003e to control how thumbs behave on collision.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(rangeSlider.machine, {\n  defaultValue: [20, 80],\n  thumbCollisionBehavior: \"push\", // \"none\" | \"push\" | \"swap\"\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eUsage within forms\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo use range slider in forms, set \u003ccode\u003ename\u003c/code\u003e and render\n\u003ccode\u003eapi.getHiddenInputProps({ index })\u003c/code\u003e for each thumb.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(rangeSlider.machine, {\n  name: \"quantity\",\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eRTL Support\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe slider has built-in support for RTL alignment and interaction. In the RTL\nmode, operations are performed from right to left, meaning, the left arrow key\nwill increment and the right arrow key will decrement.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo enable RTL support, pass the \u003ccode\u003edir: rtl\u003c/code\u003e context property\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(rangeSlider.machine, {\n  dir: \"rtl\",\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhile we take care of the interactions in RTL mode, you'll have to ensure you\napply the correct CSS styles to flip the layout.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eStyling guide\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eEach slider part includes a \u003ccode\u003edata-part\u003c/code\u003e attribute you can target in CSS.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eFocused State\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen the slider thumb is focused, the \u003ccode\u003edata-focus\u003c/code\u003e attribute is added to the\nroot, control, thumb and label parts.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-css\"\u003e[data-part=\"root\"][data-focus] {\n  /* styles for root focus state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"thumb\"]:focus {\n  /* styles for thumb focus state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"control\"][data-focus] {\n  /* styles for control focus state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"track\"][data-focus] {\n  /* styles for track focus state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"range\"][data-focus] {\n  /* styles for range focus state */\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eDisabled State\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen the slider is disabled, the \u003ccode\u003edata-disabled\u003c/code\u003e attribute is added to the root,\nlabel, control and thumb.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-css\"\u003e[data-part=\"root\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for root disabled state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"label\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for label disabled state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"control\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for control disabled state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"value-text\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for output disabled state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"thumb\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for thumb disabled state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"range\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for range disabled state */\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eOrientation\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-css\"\u003e[data-part=\"root\"][data-orientation=\"(horizontal|vertical)\"] {\n  /* styles for horizontal or vertical  */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"thumb\"][data-orientation=\"(horizontal|vertical)\"] {\n  /* styles for horizontal or vertical  */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"track\"][data-orientation=\"(horizontal|vertical)\"] {\n  /* styles for horizontal or vertical  */\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eMethods and Properties\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eMachine Context\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe slider likely forgot to import, pass, or provide it.\")}"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"12:T1adf,"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"A range slider is a multi-thumb slider used to select a range between two\nnumbers.\n\n\u003cResources pkg=\"@zag-js/slider\" /\u003e\n\n\u003cShowcase id=\"RangeSlider\" /\u003e\n\n**Features**\n\n- Fully managed keyboard navigation\n- Supports touch or click on track to update value\n- Supports Right-to-Left directionality\n- Supports horizontal and vertical orientations\n- Prevents text selection while dragging\n\n## Installation\n\nInstall the range slider package:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"range-slider/installation.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\nCheck the slider anatomy and part names.\n\n\u003e Each part includes a `data-part` attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"slider\" /\u003e\n\n## Usage\n\nImport the range slider package:\n\n```jsx\nimport * as rangeSlider from \"@zag-js/slider\"\n```\n\nThe range slider package exports two key functions:\n\n- `machine` - State machine logic.\n- `connect` - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\n\n\u003e Pass a unique `id` to `useMachine` so generated element ids stay predictable.\n\nThen use the framework integration helpers:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"range-slider/usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Changing the orientation\n\nBy default, the slider is assumed to be horizontal. To change the orientation to\nvertical, set the `orientation` property in the machine's context to `vertical`.\n\nIn this mode, the slider will use the arrow up and down keys to\nincrement/decrement its value.\n\n\u003e Don't forget to change the styles of the vertical slider by specifying its\n\u003e height\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(rangeSlider.machine, {\n  orientation: \"vertical\",\n})\n```\n\n## Setting the initial value\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(rangeSlider.machine, {\n  defaultValue: [30, 60],\n})\n```\n\n## Controlled range value\n\nUse `value` and `onValueChange` to control both thumb values externally.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(rangeSlider.machine, {\n  value,\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    setValue(details.value)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n## Specifying the minimum and maximum\n\nBy default, the minimum is `0` and the maximum is `100`. If that's not what you\nwant, you can easily specify different bounds by changing the values of the min\nand/or max attributes.\n\nFor example, to ask the user for a value between `-10` and `10`, you can use:\n\n```jsx {2-3}\nconst service = useMachine(rangeSlider.machine, {\n  min: -10,\n  max: 10,\n})\n```\n\n## Setting the value's granularity\n\nBy default, the granularity, is `1`, meaning that the value is always an\ninteger. You can change the step attribute to control the granularity.\n\nFor example, If you need a value between `5` and `10`, accurate to two decimal\nplaces, you should set the value of step to `0.01`:\n\n```jsx {4}\nconst service = useMachine(rangeSlider.machine, {\n  min: 5,\n  max: 10,\n  step: 0.01,\n})\n```\n\n## Listening for changes\n\nWhen the slider value changes, the `onValueChange` and `onValueChangeEnd`\ncallbacks are invoked. You can use this to setup custom behaviors in your app.\n\n```jsx {2-7}\nconst service = useMachine(rangeSlider.machine, {\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: number[] }\n    console.log(\"value changing to:\", details.value)\n  },\n  onValueChangeEnd(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: number[] }\n    console.log(\"value has changed to:\", details.value)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n## Listening for thumb focus changes\n\nUse `onFocusChange` to track which thumb is currently focused.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(rangeSlider.machine, {\n  onFocusChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { focusedIndex: number, value: number[] }\n    console.log(\"focused thumb:\", details.focusedIndex)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n## Preventing thumb overlap\n\nBy default, the range slider thumbs are allowed to overlap when their values are\nequal. To prevent this, use the `minStepsBetweenThumbs` to avoid thumbs with\nequal values.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(rangeSlider.machine, {\n  minStepsBetweenThumbs: 1,\n})\n```\n\n## Thumb collision behavior\n\nUse `thumbCollisionBehavior` to control how thumbs behave on collision.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(rangeSlider.machine, {\n  defaultValue: [20, 80],\n  thumbCollisionBehavior: \"push\", // \"none\" | \"push\" | \"swap\"\n})\n```\n\n## Usage within forms\n\nTo use range slider in forms, set `name` and render\n`api.getHiddenInputProps({ index })` for each thumb.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(rangeSlider.machine, {\n  name: \"quantity\",\n})\n```\n\n## RTL Support\n\nThe slider has built-in support for RTL alignment and interaction. In the RTL\nmode, operations are performed from right to left, meaning, the left arrow key\nwill increment and the right arrow key will decrement.\n\nTo enable RTL support, pass the `dir: rtl` context property\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(rangeSlider.machine, {\n  dir: \"rtl\",\n})\n```\n\n\u003e While we take care of the interactions in RTL mode, you'll have to ensure you\n\u003e apply the correct CSS styles to flip the layout.\n\n## Styling guide\n\nEach slider part includes a `data-part` attribute you can target in CSS.\n\n### Focused State\n\nWhen the slider thumb is focused, the `data-focus` attribute is added to the\nroot, control, thumb and label parts.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"root\"][data-focus] {\n  /* styles for root focus state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"thumb\"]:focus {\n  /* styles for thumb focus state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"control\"][data-focus] {\n  /* styles for control focus state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"track\"][data-focus] {\n  /* styles for track focus state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"range\"][data-focus] {\n  /* styles for range focus state */\n}\n```\n\n### Disabled State\n\nWhen the slider is disabled, the `data-disabled` attribute is added to the root,\nlabel, control and thumb.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"root\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for root disabled state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"label\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for label disabled state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"control\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for control disabled state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"value-text\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for output disabled state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"thumb\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for thumb disabled state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"range\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for range disabled state */\n}\n```\n\n### Orientation\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"root\"][data-orientation=\"(horizontal|vertical)\"] {\n  /* styles for horizontal or vertical  */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"thumb\"][data-orientation=\"(horizontal|vertical)\"] {\n  /* styles for horizontal or vertical  */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"track\"][data-orientation=\"(horizontal|vertical)\"] {\n  /* styles for horizontal or vertical  */\n}\n```\n\n## Methods and Properties\n\n### Machine Context\n\nThe slider machine exposes the following context properties:\n\n\u003cContextTable name=\"slider\" /\u003e\n\n### Machine API\n\nThe slider `api` exposes the following methods:\n\n\u003cApiTable name=\"slider\" /\u003e\n\n### Data Attributes\n\n\u003cDataAttrTable name=\"slider\" /\u003e\n\n## Accessibility\n\nAdheres to the\n[Slider WAI-ARIA design pattern](https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/slidertwothumb).\n\n### Keyboard Interactions\n\n\u003cKeyboardTable name=\"range-slider\" /\u003e"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"5:[\"$\",\"$Le\",null,{\"doc\":{\"title\":\"Range Slider\",\"description\":\"Using the range slider machine in your
